date: "2018-06-30"
categories: type-theory

toc: true
---

We want to formilise in HoTT the intuition behind a correspondance between the
concept of PathOver and total spaces. PathOver was briefly mentioned in
{% cite hottbook %} and later defined in {% cite Licata2015 %}.

![](/assets/png-images/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers-7f9fb342.png)

Since pathovers are common in HoTT (See for instance its extensive use in {%
cite hott-in:agda %}), the following stregthen our intution about these types.
Let's review the equility types (See {% cite Licata2015 %}).

## Homogeneous equality

> `Path {A} a₀ a₁` is sometimes called **homogeneous equality**, because it
> relates two elements a₀ and a₁ whose types are *definitionally/judgementally
> equal*.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="977" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="983" class="Number">30</a> <a id="986" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#996" class="Datatype Operator">_==_</a>

## Heterogeneous equality

> In {%cite McBride2004 %} the author introduced a *heterogeneous equality*, which is an equality type
> `a:A= b:B` that relates two elements `a:A` and `b:B` which may have two judgementally
> distinct types, though the reflexivity constructor applies only when both the
> two types and the two terms are judgementally equal.

> However, McBride’s heterogeneous equality is **logically equivalent** to a
> homogeneous equality type *satisfying uniqueness of identity proofs*, which
> is undesirable **in homotopy type theory, because not all types should be sets**.

> This heterogeneous equality relates two elements of two different types along a
> specific equality α between the types

  <a id="Transport-Properties.transport-concat-r"></a><a id="4786" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#4786" <a id="8885" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="8892" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8892" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="8901" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8902" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8902" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="8905" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8905" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="8907" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8909" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8910" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8910" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8912" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8914" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8919" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8902" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="8921" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8923" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8924" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8924" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="8926" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8910" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8930" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8932" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8937" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8905" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="8939" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8941" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="8949" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="9027" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="9067" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9067" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="9076" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9078" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9079" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9079" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9081" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9081" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9083" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9085" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="9087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9087" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9089" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9091" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8910" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9092" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9094" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9096" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8924" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9098" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9087" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9099" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9102" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9104" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9109" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9110" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8902" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="9113" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9115" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#8905" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9117" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="10161" class="Comment">-- The fiber of a map over a point is given by</a>

  <a id="10605" class="Comment">-- Contractible types. A contractible type is a type such that every</a>
  <a id="10676" class="Comment">-- element is equal to a center of contraction.</a>

<a id="10809" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="10814" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10583" class="Module">Contractible</a> <a id="10827" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="10835" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Equivalence"></a><a id="10842" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10842" class="Module">Equivalence</a> <a id="10854" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="10863" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DefinitionOfEquivalence"></a><a id="10870" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10870" class="Module">DefinitionOfEquivalence</a> <a id="10894" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10895" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10895" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="10898" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10898" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="10900" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10902" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10903" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10903" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="10905" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10907" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="10912" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10895" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="10914" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10916" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10917" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10917" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="10919" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10921" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="10926" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10898" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="10928" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10930" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="10940" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="11008" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="11073" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="11090" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#11090" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="11101" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11103" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11104" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#11104" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11106" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11108" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10903" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11110" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11112" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10917" class="Bound">B</a><a id="11113" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11115" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11117" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="11122" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11123" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10895" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="11126" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="11128" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10898" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="11130" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="11136" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#11090" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="11147" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#11147" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11149" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11151" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11152" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#11152" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="11154" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11156" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10917" class="Bound">B</a><a id="11157" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11159" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11161" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10726" class="Function">isContr</a> <a id="11169" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11170" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10210" class="Function">fib</a> <a id="11174" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#11147" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11176" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#11152" class="Bound">b</a><a id="11177" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="11184" class="Comment">-- There exists an equivalence between two types if there exists a</a>
    <a id="11255" class="Comment">-- contractible function between them.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isEquiv"></a><a id="11298" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#11298" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="11306" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11308" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11309" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#11309" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11311" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11313" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10903" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11315" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11317" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10917" class="Bound">B</a><a id="11318" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11320" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11322" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="11327" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11328" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10895" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="11331" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="11333" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10898" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="11335" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="14525" class="Comment">-- equivalent to equality of the two pairs.</a>

  <a id="15527" class="Comment">-- The dependent function type to proposition types is itself a</a>
  <a id="15593" class="Comment">-- proposition.</a>

### Equivalent Types

Let be `α : A == B`, `a : A`, and `b : B` then the following types are equivalent
to `HEq`.

- `T1: Path (coe α a) b`

<a id="27140" class="Comment">-- T1-≃-HEq : ∀ {ℓ} (A : Type ℓ) → (B : Type ℓ) (α : A == B)(a : A)(b : B)</a>
<a id="27215" class="Comment">--     → T1 A B α a b ≃ HEq A B α a b</a>
<a id="27253" class="Comment">-- T1-≃-HEq A .A idp a b = ( T1-to-HEq A A idp a b , isequiv)</a>
<a id="27315" class="Comment">--   where</a>
<a id="27326" class="Comment">--     isequiv : isEquiv (T1-to-HEq A A idp a b)</a>
<a id="27375" class="Comment">--     isequiv hid = ( ( idp , idp) , λ x → {!  !})</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<a id="27801" class="Comment">-- ≅-to-≡ : ∀ {ℓ} {A : Set ℓ} {B : Set ℓ} {α : A == B}{a : A}{b : B} → HEq A B α a b → a == b</a>
<a id="27895" class="Comment">-- ≅-to-≡ = {!   !}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

- <pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28822" class="Comment">-- pathover defined by path induction</a>

<a id="28977" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28860" class="Function">PathOver₅</a> <a id="28987" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28988" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="28990" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28992" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28992" class="Bound">A</a><a id="28993" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28995" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28995" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28997" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1047" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="29001" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29001" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="29004" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29004" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="29007" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29009" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29001" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="29012" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#996" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="29015" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29004" class="Bound">c₂</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Above when we used `transport C α c₁`, we could also have used `coe (ap C α)`,
both functions are of type `C a₁ → C a₂`. The other case with c₂ is similar.

We are going to use the fifth definition for pathovers, the one which is
using an inductive family.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="29301" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29301" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="29310" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29312" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28860" class="Function">PathOver₅</a>

<a id="29323" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="29329" class="Number">30</a> <a id="29332" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29301" class="Function">PathOver</a>
<a id="29341" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="29348" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29301" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="29365" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>



> While we have motivated PathOver as a factored heteroge- neous equality, there
> is also a geometric intuition. Dependent types correspond to fibrations, so a
> type C : A ? Type can be pictured as its total space Σ a:A. C a projecting down
> to A by first projection. A path-over γ : PathOver C α c1 c2 represents a path σ
> in Σ a:A. C a between (a1,c1) and (a2,c2), such that ap fst σ is exactly α. That
> is, it is a path in the total space that projects down to, or lies over, α (path
> pairing pair= αγ will be made precise below)


## Total spaces

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="29969" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="29976" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29976" class="Module">_</a> <a id="29978" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29979" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29979" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="29981" href="{% endraw %}{% _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29984" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="29986" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29988" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="29993" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29979" class="Bound">i</a><a id="29994" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="29996" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29996" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="29998" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30000" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29984" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="30002" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30004" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#712" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="30009" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29981" class="Bound">j</a><a id="30010" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="30012" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#30012" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="30014" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers.md %}{% raw
